				<h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading pagetitle page-header">
					String Quartet in G minor, Hob.III:33 (Haydn, Joseph)				</h1>

</td></tr>

<th>Genre Categories<span class="addpagetag mh555"></span>
</th>

</th>
<td class="wi_head" style="width:100%">String Quartet in G minor
</td></tr>
<tr>

</th>
<td class="wi_head">String Quartet No.33&#160;; "Sun Quartet No.3"

</td></tr>
<tr>

</th>
<td>4 movements
<ol><li>Allegro con spirito (G minor)
</li><li>Minuet. Allegretto (B-flat major) - Trio (E-flat major)
</li><li>Poco adagio (G major)
</li><li>Allegro molto (G minor)
</li></ol>
</td></tr>
